// assignment[i] == 0 means card i is unused.
// assignment[i] == j (1 <= j <= k) means card i belongs to phone number j.

{

  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&

}

    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)

ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
    invariant 0 <= cnt8 <= |digits|
  {
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }

  assert Achievable(count, digits);
  assert !Achievable(count + 1, digits);
}

  }

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
    invariant 0 <= cnt8 <= i
  {
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
}

// Count occurrences of value v in sequence s
ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

// Formalizes the problem statement: a valid assignment of cards to k phone numbers.
// assignment[i] == 0 means card i is unused.
// assignment[i] == j (1 <= j <= k) means card i belongs to phone number j.
// Each phone number uses exactly 11 cards, at least one of which has digit 8
// (capturing: phone numbers have length 11 and start with 8).
ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

// Necessary and sufficient condition for forming k phone numbers from the cards:
//   - Each phone number requires 11 cards  =>  11 * k <= |digits|
//   - Each phone number requires at least one 8  =>  k <= count of 8s
ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {

    count := n / 11;

  assert 11 * count <= |digits|;
  assert count <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8);

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
    invariant 0 <= cnt8 <= |digits|
  {
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
}

ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

// Formalizes the problem statement: a valid assignment of cards to k phone numbers.
// assignment[i] == 0 means card i is unused.
// assignment[i] == j (1 <= j <= k) means card i belongs to phone number j.
// Each phone number uses exactly 11 cards, at least one of which has digit 8
// (capturing: phone numbers have length 11 and start with 8).
ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

// Necessary and sufficient condition for forming k phone numbers from the cards:
//   - Each phone number requires 11 cards  =>  11 * k <= |digits|
//   - Each phone number requires at least one 8  =>  k <= count of 8s
ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
  {
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
}

  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
  {
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }
  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
}

{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&

  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::

    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

}

  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|

    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);

// Count occurrences of value v in sequence s
ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

// Formalizes the problem statement: a valid assignment of cards to k phone numbers.
// assignment[i] == 0 means card i is unused.
// assignment[i] == j (1 <= j <= k) means card i belongs to phone number j.
// Each phone number uses exactly 11 cards, at least one of which has digit 8
// (capturing: phone numbers have length 11 and s...

--- LLM RESPONSE (444 tokens, 3.16s) ---
<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
    invariant 0 <= i <= |digits|
  {

    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
}

ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
  {

    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  assert CountOccurrences(digits, 8) == cnt8;

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
}

// Count occurrences of value v in sequence s

// assignment[i] == 0 means card i is unused.

--- LLM RESPONSE (575 tokens, 8.05s) ---
<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

// Formalizes the problem statement: a valid assignment of cards to k phone numbers.
// assignment[i] == 0 means card i is unused.
// assignment[i] == j (1 <= j <= k) means card i belongs to phone number j.
// Each phone number uses exactly 11 cards, at least one of which has digit 8
// (capturing: phone numbers have length 11 and start with 8).
ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

// Necessary and sufficient condition for forming k phone numbers from the cards:
//   - Each phone number requires 11 cards  =>  11 * k <= |digits|
//   - Each phone number requires at least one 8  =>  k <= count of 8s
ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
  {
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
}

  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

// Formalizes the problem statement: a valid assignment of cards to k phone numbers.
// assignment[i] == 0 means card i is unused.
// assignment[i] == j (1 <= j <= k) means card i belongs to phone number j.
// Each phone number uses exactly 11 cards, at least one of which has digit 8
// (capturing: phone numbers have length 11 and start with 8).
ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

// Necessary and sufficient condition for forming k phone numbers from the cards:
//   - Each phone number requires 11 cards  =>  11 * k <= |digits|
//   - Each phone number requires at least...

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
    invariant 0 <= cnt8 <= |digits|
  {
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  assert cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits, 8);
  assert n == |digits|;
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
  assert Achievable(count, digits);
  assert !Achievable(count + 1, digits);
}

ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
    invariant 0 <= cnt8 <= n
  {
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
  assert Achievable(count, digits);

    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))

//   - Each phone number requires 11 cards  =>  11 * k <= |digits|
//   - Each phone number requires at least one 8  =>  k <= count of 8s

ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
  {
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
}

  decreases |s|
{

}

// assignment[i] == 0 means card i is unused.
// assignment[i] == j (1 <= j <= k) means card i belongs to phone number j.

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
  {
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
}

// Count occurrences of value v in sequence s
ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

// Formalizes the problem statement: a valid assignment of cards to k phone numbers.
// assignment[i] == 0 means card i is unused.
// assignment[i] == j (1 <= j <= k) means card i belongs to phone number j.
// Each phone number uses exactly 11 cards, at least one of which has digit 8
// (capturing: phone numbers have length 11 and start with 8).
ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

// Necessary and sufficient condition for forming k phone numbers from the cards:
//   - Each phone number requires 11 cards  =>  11 * k <= |digits|
//   - Each phone number requires at least one 8  =>  k <= count of 8s
ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

{

  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
  {
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
}

  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
  {
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
  assert Achievable(count, digits);
  assert !Achievable(count + 1, digits);
}

ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

// Formalizes the problem statement: a valid assignment of cards to k phone numbers.
// assignment[i] == 0 means card i is unused.
// assignment[i] == j (1 <= j <= k) means card i belongs to phone number j.
// Each phone number uses exactly 11 cards, at least one of which has digit 8
// (capturing: phone numbers have length 11 and start with 8).

{

  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

//   - Each phone number requires at least one 8  =>  k <= count of 8s

{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

// Formalizes the problem statement: a valid assignment of cards to k phone numbers.
// assignment[i] == 0 means card i is unused.
// assignment[i] == j (1 <= j <= k) means card i belongs to phone number j.
// Each phone number uses exactly 11 cards, at least one of which has digit 8
// (capturing: phone numbers have length 11 and start with 8).
ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

// Necessary and sufficient condition for forming k phone numbers from the cards:
//   - Each phone number requires 11 cards  =>  11 * k <= |digits|
//   - Each phone number requires at least one 8  =>  k <= count of 8s
ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n ...

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
    invariant 0 <= i <= |digits|
    invariant CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8) <= i
  {
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  assert cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
  assert count <= n / 11;
  assert count <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8);
  assert 11 * count <= |digits|;
  assert Achievable(count, digits);
  assert !Achievable(count + 1, digits);
}

ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
  {
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
}

// Count occurrences of value v in sequence s
ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

// Formalizes the problem statement: a valid assignment of cards to k phone numbers.
// assignment[i] == 0 means card i is unused.
// assignment[i] == j (1 <= j <= k) means card i belongs to phone number j.
// Each phone number uses exactly 11 cards, at least one of which has digit 8
// (capturing: phone numbers have length 11 and start with 8).
ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

// Necessary and sufficient condition for forming k phone numbers from the cards:
//   - Each phone number requires 11 cards  =>  11 * k <= |digits|
//   - Each phone number requires at least one 8  =>  k <= count of 8s
ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }

  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
